ds-font-regular ds-uppercase ds-text-typo-mid3">Born</p><span class="ds-text-title-s ds-font-bold ds-text-typo"><p>June 08, 1991, Berbice, Guyana</p></span></div><div><p class="ds-text-tight-m ds-font-regular ds-uppercase ds-text-typo-mid3">Age</p><span class="ds-text-title-s ds-font-bold ds-text-typo"><p>33y 256d</p></span></div><div><p class="ds-text-tight-m ds-font-regular ds-uppercase ds-text-typo-mid3 ds-mb-4">TEAMS</p><div class="ds-grid lg:ds-grid-cols-3 ds-grid-cols-2 ds-gap-y-4"><a href="/team/united-states-of-america-11" title="Alex Amsterdam&#x27;s United States of America cricket team profile" class="ds-flex ds-items-center ds-space-x-4"><img width="24" height="24" alt="USA flag team logo" style="width:24px;height:24px" class="overview-teams-image" src="https://wassets.hscicdn.com/static/images/lazyimage-noaspect.svg"/><span title="United States of America" class="ds-cursor-pointer ds-inline-flex ds-items-start ds-leading-none"><span class="ds-text-title-s ds-font-bold ds-text-typo ds-underline ds-decoration-ui-stroke hover:ds-text-typo-primary hover:ds-decoration-ui-stroke-primary ds-block">United States of America</span></span></a><a href="/team/new-york-region-769109" title="Alex Amsterdam&#x27;s New York Region cricket team profile" class="ds-flex ds-items-center ds-space-x-4"><i style="font-size:20px" class="icon-shield-filled ds-text-icon-light"></i><span title="New York Region" class="ds-cursor-pointer ds-inline-flex ds-items-start ds-leading-none"><span class="ds-text-title-s ds-font-bold ds-text-typo ds-underline ds-decoration-ui-stroke hover:ds-text-typo-primary hover:ds-decoration-ui-stroke-primary ds-block">New York Region</span></span></a></div></div><div class="ds-relative ds-overflow-hidden ds-mt-6" style="height:162px"><div class="ci-player-bio-content"><p>A technically sound left-handed batsman, Alex Amsterdam represented his native Guyana at the Under-19 level in 2009 but by the following year he had moved to New York. Qualifying to play for USA under the ICC's four-year residency guidelines, he made his USA debut at the 2015 World T20 Qualifier in Ireland.</p><p>Amsterdam was subsequently picked for a combined ICC Americas squad of USA and Canada players to go to Trinidad & Tobago for the 2016 WICB Nagico Super50 competition. His experience in the Caribbean from his junior days came through as he made 73 off 87 balls on List A debut against Barbados. He is utilised from time to time to bowl part-time offbreaks and is a sure-handed fielder.<br>
